decisions = {
# Werewolf Gifts
# All Werewolves have affinity with Father Wolf and Mother Moon gifts. (Including Pure)
# All auspice-only gifts are affinity for that auspice.
# Rahu- Dominance, Strength,
# Blood Talons- Inspiration, Rage, Strength, Battle (Rage)
# Bone Shadows- Death, Insight, Warding, Ending(Rage)
# Cahalith- Inspiration, Knowledge
# Hunters in Darkness- Elemental, Nature, Stealth, Stalking(Rage)
# Iron Masters-Knowledge, Shaping, Technology, Blending(Rage)
# Elodoth-Insight, Warding
# Irraka-Evasion, Stealth
# Storm Lords-Dominance, Evasion, Weather, Alpha (Rage)
# Ithaeur-Elemental, Shaping
# Fire-Touched- Disease, Ferver, Insight, Inspiration
# Ivory Claws-Agony, Dominance, Scourging, Warding
# Predator Kings-Nature, Rage, Savagery, Strength


open_gift_training_menu = {
	is_high_prio = yes
	potential = {
			trait = werewolf NOT = { OR = { has_character_flag = disciplines_menu_open  has_character_flag = abilities_menu_open} }
			NOT = { has_character_flag = gifts_menu_open }
			ai = no
	}
	allow = {
		age = 50
	}
	effect = { set_character_flag = gifts_menu_open }
	ai_will_do = { factor = 0 }
}
close_gift_training_menu = {
	is_high_prio = yes
	potential = {
			trait = werewolf NOT = { OR= { has_character_flag = disciplines_menu_open  has_character_flag = abilities_menu_open} }
			has_character_flag = gifts_menu_open 
			ai = no
	}
	allow = {
		age = 50
	}
	effect = { clr_character_flag = gifts_menu_open }
	ai_will_do = { factor = 0 }
}
train_gift_Agony_1_decision = {
	potential = { OR = { ai =yes    has_character_flag = gifts_menu_open } 
			trait = werewolf NOT = { OR= { has_character_flag = disciplines_menu_open  has_character_flag = abilities_menu_open} }
			religion = ivory_claws
			NOT = { has_character_flag = POD_LEARNING_WEREWOLF_GIFT }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Agony_1 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Agony_2 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Agony_3 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Agony_4 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Agony_5 }
	}
	allow = {
		prestige = 100
	}
	effect = {
		prestige = -100
		add_trait = gift_Agony_1
		# in clan bonus
	}
	ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = { factor = 0.04  
			}
			modifier = { factor = 0
							NOT = { martial = 10 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2
					religion = ivory_claws }
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					OR = {
							trait = misguided_warrior 
							trait = tough_soldier 
							trait = skilled_tactician 
							trait = brilliant_strategist
							trait = duelist
						}
					}
			}
}

train_gift_Alpha_1_decision = {
	potential = { OR = { ai =yes    has_character_flag = gifts_menu_open }
			trait = werewolf NOT = { OR= { has_character_flag = disciplines_menu_open  has_character_flag = abilities_menu_open} }
			religion = storm_lords
			NOT = { has_character_flag = POD_LEARNING_WEREWOLF_GIFT }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Alpha_1 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Alpha_2 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Alpha_3 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Alpha_4 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Alpha_5 }
	}
	allow = {
		prestige = 100
	}
	effect = {
		prestige = -100
		add_trait = gift_Alpha_1
	}
	ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = { factor = 0.04   
			}
			modifier = { factor = 0
							NOT = { diplomacy = 10 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2
					religion = storm_lords }
								modifier = {
										factor = 2
										OR = {	
												trait = naive_appeaser 
												trait = underhanded_rogue 
												trait = charismatic_negotiator
												trait = grey_eminence 
												}
											}	
			}
}

train_gift_Bone_1_decision = {
	potential = { OR = { ai =yes    has_character_flag = gifts_menu_open }
			trait = werewolf NOT = { OR= { has_character_flag = disciplines_menu_open  has_character_flag = abilities_menu_open} }
			NOT = { has_character_flag = POD_LEARNING_WEREWOLF_GIFT }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Bone_1 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Bone_2 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Bone_3 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Bone_4 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Bone_5 }
	}
	allow = {
		prestige = 100	
	}
	effect = {
		prestige = -100
		add_trait = gift_Bone_1
		# in clan bonus
		if = { limit = { OR = {
						trait = auspice_rahu 
						religion = storm_lords
						}}
				prestige = 5
				}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = { factor = 0.04   
			}
			modifier = { factor = 0
							NOT = { learning = 10 } }
			modifier = { factor = 0
							NOT = { martial = 10 } }				
								modifier = {
										factor = 2
										OR = {	
												trait = detached_priest 
												trait = martial_cleric 
												trait = scholarly_theologian 
												trait = mastermind_theologian
												trait = misguided_warrior 
												trait = tough_soldier 
												trait = skilled_tactician 
												trait = brilliant_strategist
												trait = duelist												
														}
													}					
			}
}

			trait = werewolf NOT = { OR= { has_character_flag = disciplines_menu_open  has_character_flag = abilities_menu_open} }
			trait = auspice_elodoth
			NOT = { has_character_flag = POD_LEARNING_WEREWOLF_GIFT }
			trait = gift_Judges_Moon_4 
	}
	allow = {
		prestige = 1000
	}
	effect = {
		prestige = -1000
		add_trait = gift_Judges_Moon_5
	}
	ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = { factor = 0.04   
			}
			modifier = { factor = 2
					trait = auspice_elodoth }					
								modifier = {
										factor = 2
										OR = {	
												trait = misguided_warrior 
												trait = tough_soldier 
												trait = skilled_tactician 
												trait = brilliant_strategist
												trait = duelist										
												trait = naive_appeaser 
												trait = underhanded_rogue 
												trait = charismatic_negotiator
												trait = grey_eminence 
												}
											}
			}
}
train_gift_Knowledge_1_decision = {
	potential = { OR = { ai =yes    has_character_flag = gifts_menu_open }
			trait = werewolf NOT = { OR= { has_character_flag = disciplines_menu_open  has_character_flag = abilities_menu_open} }
			OR = {
					trait = auspice_cahalith
					religion = iron_masters
			}
			NOT = { has_character_flag = POD_LEARNING_WEREWOLF_GIFT }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Knowledge_1 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Knowledge_2 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Knowledge_3 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Knowledge_4 }
			NOT = { trait = gift_Knowledge_5 }
	}
	allow = {
		prestige = 100
	}
	effect = {
		prestige = -100
		add_trait = gift_Knowledge_1
	}
	ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = { factor = 0.04   
			}
			modifier = { factor = 0
							NOT = { learning = 10 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2
					trait = auspice_cahalith }
			modifier = { factor = 2
					religion = iron_masters }					
								modifier = {
										factor = 2
										OR = {	
												trait = detached_priest 
												trait = martial_cleric 
												trait = scholarly_theologian 
												trait = mastermind_theologian
														}
													}
			}
}
